<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мудрить.html>мудри́ть</a> (25494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мудрый.html>му́дрый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múdryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мудрить.html>мудри́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mudrítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">намудри́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">смудри́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be too clever, to complicate things unnecessarily</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">― <a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>Ведь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:мудрость.html>му́дрость</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>кака́я</a>, ― <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:петрушка.html>Петру́шка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>глядя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искоса.html>и́скоса</a>, ― окроме <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>, спустясь <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>горы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> попрямей, <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> больше <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><a href = vnd.unilang:мудрый.html>му́дрое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высказывание.html>выска́зывание</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:суждение.html>сужде́ние</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

</ul></li>

***мудрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мудрый.html>му́дрый</a> (3302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мудръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mudrŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫdrъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*mandras</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">mandrùs</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mundraz</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">munter</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мудрый.html>му́дрый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múdryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мудре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мудре́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тренер.html>тре́неры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молоды́е</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мудрый.html>му́дрые</a></b>.</i><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://24news.ru/news/sports/895894773s.html">[1]</a><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Trénery u komándy molodýje, no užé <b>múdryje</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The team's trainers are young, but are already wise.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***муж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> муж (432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫžь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mon-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">man</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужество.html>му́жество</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múžestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужественный.html>му́жественный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múžestvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)му́жественнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)му́жественней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>manly, virile, masculine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having the characteristics of a man</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:женственный.html>же́нственный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žénstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>courageous, brave, gutsy
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:храбрый.html>хра́брый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xrábryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трусливый.html>трусли́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">truslívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мужик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужи́к</a> (655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">муж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muž</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">man (dated); husband</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужи́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mužík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boor</li>
<li>coarse, uncouth person</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial or derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> man (male person)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> husband</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> peasant from tsarist Russia</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> macho</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> (1789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">муж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muž</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">man</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ско́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mužskój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>male</li>
<li>masculine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mužskój</b> rod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">masculine gender</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>man's, gentleman's</li></ol>

***мужчина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́на</a> (410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested since the 16th century as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мущи́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muščína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; the word is still pronounced in a way that is directly rendered by this outdated spelling, but the current spelling more explicitly displays the etymology and the even older Slavic sound structure. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*мѫжьщина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*mǫžĭščina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫžьščina</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫžьskъ</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ina</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫžь</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьskъ</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mužskój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mužčína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>man</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">muzeum</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Museum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mūsēum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μουσεῖον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mouseîon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">му́зика</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múzyka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">muzyka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">muzika</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">musica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μουσική</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mousikḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múzyka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зык</a></b>)

<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бетхо́вен</span>  | Beethoven | ”, performed by <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Сплин</span> (Splean):</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">бетхо́вен <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жив</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:музыка.html>му́зыка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лети́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этаж.html>этажи́</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прекрасный.html>прекра́сна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Betxóven živ i <b>múzyka</b> letít skvozʹ etaží<br />Sevódnja útrom tak prekrásna žiznʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Beethoven is alive and the music is flying through the floors<br />So beautiful is life this morning</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:музыкальный.html>музыкально</a> (26949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***мука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>мука</a> (2616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǭka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh"><a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>мука</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">muka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">meal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">moka</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">múka</i>. Non-Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μάσσω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mássō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">mengen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>мука́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">muká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>муки́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучной.html>мучно́й</a></b>) <i>(mass noun, no plural)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>flour, fine meal</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мукомол.html>мукомо́л</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mukomól</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мучни́стый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mučnístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">torment, torture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>мулла́</a> (22671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>мулла́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mulla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مولى</i> | . Attested since 17th century.
</p><p>Replaced earlier (16th – 18th cc.) <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">молла</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>мулла́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mullá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>муллы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>муллы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мулла.html>мулл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Islam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mullah (<i>a Muslim religious scholar and teacher</i>)</li></ol>

***мумия.html

***мундир.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мундир.html>мунди́р</a> (4381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">mundur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Montur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">monture</i> (see there for more) and perhaps influenced by “mondiren”, an earlier form of the German verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">montieren</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мундир.html>мунди́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mundír</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мундир.html>мунди́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мундир.html>мунди́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мундир.html>мунди́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(military) uniform
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:картофель.html>карто́фель</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:картошка.html>карто́шка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мундир.html>мунди́ре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kartófelʹ/kartóška v <b>mundíre</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(young) potatoes in their jackets / skin</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мура.html>мура́</a> (12184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mura</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*murъ</i> and further with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">mauras</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мура.html>мура́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">murá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мура.html>муры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nonsense, garbage, rubbish</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ерунда.html>ерунда́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jerundá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупость.html>глу́пость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">glúpostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чепуха.html>чепуха́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čepuxá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустяк.html>пустя́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pustják</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">безде́лица</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bezdélica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бессмыслица.html>бессмы́слица</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bessmýslica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чушь.html>чушь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čušʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***муравей.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>мураве́й</a> (6712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*morvъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*MorwiH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>мураве́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">muravéj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>муравья́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>муравьи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>муравьёв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate or inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a special motor scooter with three wheels and a rear cargo area made in the USSR between 1959 and 1995 in Tula, officially capitalised - <a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>Мураве́й</a>, some models were given different names: <a href = vnd.unilang:турист.html>Тури́ст</a>, Тулица, the first model's name was <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тула.html>ту́ла</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Túla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1996</b>,  Valentin Kononov, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> добря́га Сёмка <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спа́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> ре́йса <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>муравье́</a></b>» <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лал</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I poká dobrjága Sjómka spal, ja tri réjsa na “<b>muravʹjé</b>” sdélal.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And while the good Syomka slept, I made three trips on my "<b>ant</b>".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1996</b>,  <cite>Moskva</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Дак <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переломанный.html>перело́мано</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>муравье́</a></b>» <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грузовик.html>грузовико́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:столкнуться.html>столкну́лся</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dak vsjó ž perelómano. On že na “<b>muravʹjé</b>” s gruzovikóm stolknúlsja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Why, everything is shattered. You see, his "<b>ant</b>" has collided with a truck.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  William Gibson, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотрудник.html>сотру́дники</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́него</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>муравья́</a></b>»?</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A móžet, éto býli sotrúdniki “Sínevo <b>muravʹjá</b>”?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Or maybe they were officers from the "Blue <b>ant</b>"?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>As the name of the motor scooter, the term is often written in lower case as a friendly, jocular term. It's also often used as an animate noun like an "ant" (insect) (insects are animate nouns in Russian when they are used in the direct sense).</li></ul>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">muravéjnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравьиный.html>муравьи́ный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">muravʹínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йник</a> (11509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравей.html>мураве́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muravéj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">muravéjnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>anthill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> apartment building or high-rise
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b> October 30,  “Новости <a href = vnd.unilang:строительство.html>строи́тельства</a> Санкт-Петербурга”, in  <cite>Канонер</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://kanoner.com/2015/10/30/147732/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a> Беринга, 29, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:построенный.html>постро́ен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилой.html>жилой</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:муравейник.html>мураве́йник</a></b>», <a href = vnd.unilang:оформленный.html>офо́рмленный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нтам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостиница.html>гости́ница</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступающий.html>выступа́ющим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоджия.html>ло́джиям</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напомнить.html>напо́мнит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конструктор.html>констру́ктор</a> лего.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na úlice Beringa, 29, búdet postrójen žiloj “<b>muravéjnik</b>”, ofórmlennyj po dokuméntam kak gostínica. Blagodarjá vystupájuščim lódžijam on napómnit konstrúktor lego.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A residential <b>high-rise</b> will be built at 29 Beringa Street. Registered as a hotel, it resembles a Lego set thanks to its projecting loggias.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
